# Major dates in Khyan History

# SA 800 - Khyan Migration over the Gap

# TA 1064 - 5097.9.1 - Empire proclaimed by Dârayavahu I after the unification of the Khyan Heartland.
# TA 1110 - 5143.8.23 - Arysis conquered by Xshayârshan I.
# TA 1115 - 5148.11.11 - Mejhanir conquered by Xshayârshan I. Harshandatt would be defeated fully and made a triubtary in the next 3 years.
# TA 1148 - 5181.6.1 - Dâtuvahya I converts to the Cult of Arien and proclaims it the state religion.

# TA 1652 - 5685.2.24 - Ardacher I comes to the throne after the Great Plague decimates Khy, eradicating many families
# TA 1686 - - Ardacher I invades Anarike, bringing it under Khyan dominion
# TA 1751 - - Ardacher II conquers Sirayn, finally driving out Khorahil and establishing Khyan domination over most of the bay
# TA 1950 - 5983.5.1 - Sirayni and other revolts finally result in the assasination of Khashayar II and the start of the Century of Chaos

# TA 2050 - 6083.7.30 - Artaxshasa I solidifes control of Khy, beginning the Dark Dynasty

# TA 2372 - 6405.04.19 - Midarayân I overthrows the Dark Dynasty and purifies Khy
# TA 2516 - 6549.3.1 - Gorazehan Rebellion. A family related to the old 4th Dynasty revolts against the 5th in a bid to size power, having consolidated a great hold in the Bulchyadean Marches and Nosharud. They are ultimately defeated in 2523 ( 6556.5.17 ) with the last conspiritors exceuted or exiled.
# TA 2526 - 6559.6.21 - Khy partitions Anarike with a rising Codya, securing Kandalar and starting the Codyan Yoke.
# TA 2649 - 6682.4.1 - Xshayarshan V strenghens the miltary and fortifies the Gap of Khy, establishing many miltary governers. 

# TA 2750 - 6783.8.21 - Aldhrad I comes to the throne in a military coup, establishing the 5th dynasty
# TA 2759 - 6792.5.23 - Aldhrad I conqueres Arysis
# TA 2775 - 6808.7.13 - Artaban I 'liberates' Anarike from the Codyan Yoke
# TA 2794 - 6817.9.5 - Artaban turns north to Chey
# TA 2802 - 6835.6.1 - Khodad I invades Harshandatt and Sirayn. He is killed in battle in 2804, but his son Shoburgan II finshes the war, establishing dominion over the coastlands and Mejhanir in TA 2805 - 6838.10.14.

# TA 2900 - 6933.4.26 - Taxmaspada I overthrows Kuru II, forming the 6th dynasty. Kuru's descendants survive in an honorary role, and many outlying parts of the empire break away.
# TA 2901 - 6934.1.1 - Arysis revolts, gains complete indep in TA 2909 (6942.10.30)
# TA 2005 - 6938.3.10 - Chey Sart revolts, gaining independence in TA 2915 (6948.7.12)
# TA 2908 - 6941.12.6 - Harshandatt revolts, gains indep in TA 2912 (6945.11.09)
# TA 2010 - 6943.6.1 - Anarike granted independence as tributary due to growing minor revolts and fears of complete collapse



#### Empire of Khy ####

e_khy = {
	5097.9.1 = { #Founding of the Empire
		holder = lineofhaxamanish4 #Dârayavahu I
		government = administrative_government
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = holder
					NOT = { has_dlc_feature = roads_to_power }
				}
				holder = {
					change_government = clan_government
				}
			}
		}
		succession_laws = {
			acclamation_succession_law
		}
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = holder
					holder = { has_government = administrative_government }
				}
				set_state_faith = faith:faith_arienism
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = holder
					has_dlc_feature = royal_court
				}
				holder = {
					set_court_type = court_scholarly #The Khyans are really into philosophy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = holder
					NOT = { has_dlc_feature = roads_to_power }
				}
				holder = {
					change_government = clan_government
					add_realm_law_skip_effects = single_heir_succession_law
				}
			}
		}
	}

d_mafazat = {
    5097.9.1 = {
        liege = e_khy
        government = administrative_government
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = holder
					NOT = { has_dlc_feature = roads_to_power }
				}
				holder = {
					change_government = clan_government
				}
			}
		}
        effect = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    exists = holder
                    exists = holder.top_liege
                    holder = {
                        government_allows = administrative
                    }
                }
                holder = {
                    vassal_contract_set_obligation_level = {
                        type = administrative_themes
                        level = 2 # Military
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

		holder = lineofzorzagari19
	}
	6750.6.12 = {
		holder = lineofzorzagari20
	}
	6805.11.22 = {
		holder = lineofzorzagari22
	}
    6808.7.13 = { # Khy ends the Codyan Yoke
        liege = e_khy
		government = administrative_government
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = holder
					NOT = { has_dlc_feature = roads_to_power }
				}
				holder = {
					change_government = feudal_government
				}
			}
		}
        effect = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    exists = holder
                    exists = holder.top_liege
                    holder = {
                        government_allows = administrative
                    }
                }
                holder = {
                    vassal_contract_set_obligation_level = {
                        type = administrative_themes
                        level = 0 # Balanced
                    }
                }
            }
        }
	}
	6850.4.20 = {
		holder = lineofzorzagari23
	}
	6901.3.12 = {
		holder = lineofzorzagari25
